susnigdhapatrapallavakusumaphalānamrasurabhimadhureṣu /
sakṣīrāvraṇasaṃsthitamanojñavṛkṣeṣu cārthasiddhikaraḥ // 94.33 //
niṣpannasasyaśādvalabhavanaprāsādaharmyahariteṣu /
dhanyocchrayamaṅgalyeṣu caiva viruvan dhanāgamadaḥ // 94.34 //
gopucchasthe valmīkage 'tha vā darśanaṃ bhujaṅgasya /
sadyo jvaro mahiṣage viruvati gulme phalaṃ svalpam // 94.35 //
kāryasya vyāghātas tṛṇakūṭe vāmage 'mbusaṃsthe vā /
ūrdhvāgnipluṣṭe 'śanihate ca kāke vadho bhavati // 94.36 //
kaṇṭakimiśre saumye siddhiḥ kāryasya bhavati kalahaś ca /
kaṇṭakini bhavati kalaho vallīpariveṣṭite bandhaḥ // 94.37 //
chinnāgre 'ṅgacchedaḥ kalahaḥ śuṣkadrumasthite dhvāṃkṣe /
purataś ca pṛṣṭhato vā gomayasaṃsthe dhanaprāptiḥ // 94.38 //
mṛtapuruṣāṅgāvayavasthito 'bhiviruvan karoti mṛtyubhayam /
bhañjann asthi ca cañcvā yadi viruvaty asthibhaṅgāya // 94.39 //
rajjvasthikāṣṭhakaṇṭakiniḥsāraśiroruhānane ruvati /
bhujagagadadaṃṣṭritaskaraśastrāgnibhayāny anukramaśaḥ // 94.40 //
sitakusumāśucimāṃsānane 'rthasiddhir yathepsitā yātuḥ /
pakṣau dhunvann ūrdhvānane ca vighnaṃ muhuḥ kvaṇati // 94.41 //
yadi śṛṅkhalāṃ varatrāṃ vallīṃ vādāya vāśate bandhaḥ /
pāṣāṇasthe ca bhayaṃ kliṣṭāpūrvādhvikayutiś ca // 94.42 //
anyonyabhakṣasaṃkrāmitānane tuṣṭir uttamā bhavati /
vijñeyaḥ strīlābho dampatyor viruvator yugapat // 94.43 //
pramadāśiropagatapūrṇakumbhasaṃsthe 'ṅganārthasamprāptiḥ /
ghaṭakuṭṭane sutavipad ghaṭopahadane 'nnasamprāptiḥ // 94.44 //
skandhāvārādīnāṃ niveśasamaye ruvaṃś calatpakṣaḥ /
sūcayate 'nyatsthānaṃ niścalapakṣas tu bhayamātram // 94.45 //
praviśadbhiḥ sainyādīn sagṛdhrakaṅkair vināmiṣaṃ dhvāṃkṣaiḥ /
aviruddhais taiḥ prītir dviṣatāṃ yuddhaṃ viruddhaiś ca // 94.46 //
bandhaḥ sūkarasaṃsthe paṅkākte sūkare dvike 'rthāptiḥ /
kṣemaṃ kharoṣṭrasaṃsthe ke cit prāhur vadhaṃ tu khare // 94.47 //
vāhanalābho 'śvagate viruvaty anuyāyini kṣatajapātaḥ /
anye 'py anuvrajanto yātāraṃ kākavad vihagāḥ // 94.48 //
dvātriṃśat pravibhakte digcakre yad yathā samuddiṣṭam /
tattat tathā vidheyaṃ guṇadoṣaphalaṃ yiyāsūnām // 94.49 //
kā iti kākasya rutaṃ svanilayasaṃsthasya niṣphalaṃ proktam /
kava iti cātmaprītyai keti rute snigdhamitrāptiḥ // 94.50 //
kareti kalahaṃ kurukuru ca harṣam atha kaṭakaṭeti dadhibhaktam /
keke virutaṃ kuku vā dhanalābhaṃ yāyinaḥ prāha // 94.51 //
kharekhare pathikāgamam āha kakhākheti yāyino mṛtyum /
gamanapratiṣedhikam ā kakhalā sadyo 'bhivarṣāya // 94.52 //
kāketi vighātaḥ kākaṭīti cāhāradūṣaṇaṃ prāha /
prītyāspadaṃ kavakaveti bandham evaṃ kagākur iti // 94.53 //
karagau virute varṣaṃ guḍavat trāsāya vaḍ iti vastrāptiḥ /
kalayeti ca saṃyogaḥ śūdrasya brāhmaṇaiḥ sākam // 94.54 //
kaḍ iti phalāptiḥ phaladāhidarśanaṃ ṭaḍḍiti prahārāḥ syuḥ /
strīlābhaḥ strīti rute gaḍ iti gavāṃ puḍ iti puṣpāṇām // 94.55 //
yuddhāya ṭākuṭākv iti guhu vahnibhayaṃ kaṭekaṭe kalahaḥ /
ṭākuli ciṇṭici kekeketi puraṃ ceti doṣāya // 94.56 //
kākadvayasyāpi samānam etat phalaṃ yaduktaṃ rutaceṣṭitādyaiḥ /
patatriṇo 'nye 'pi yathaiva kāko vanyāḥ śvavac coparidaṃṣṭriṇo ye // 94.57 //
sthalasalilacarāṇāṃ vyatyayo meghakāle pracurasalilavṛṣṭyai śeṣakāle bhayāya /
madhu bhavananilīnaṃ tat karoty āśu śūnyaṃ maraṇam api ca nīlā makṣikā mūrdhni līnā // 94.58 //
vinikṣipantyaḥ salile 'ṇḍakāni pipīlikā vṛṣṭinirodham āhuḥ /
taruṃ sthalaṃ vāpi nayanti nimnād yadā tadā tāḥ kathayanti vṛṣṭim // 94.59 //
kāryaṃ tu mūlaśakune 'ntaraje tadahni vindyāt phalaṃ niyatam evam ime vicintyāḥ /
prārambhayānasamayeṣu tathā praveśe grāhyaṃ kṣutaṃ na śubhadaṃ kva cid apy uśanti // 94.60 //
śubhaṃ daśāpākam avighnasiddhiṃ mūlābhirakṣām atha vā sahāyān /
duṣṭasya saṃsiddhim anāmayatvaṃ vadanti te mānayitur nṛpasya // 94.61 //
krośād ūrdhvaṃ śakunavirutaṃ niṣphalaṃ prāhur eke tatrāniṣṭe prathamaśakune mānayet pañca ṣaṭ ca /
prāṇāyāmān nṛpatir aśubhe ṣoḍaśaiva dvitīye pratyāgacchet svabhavanam ato yady aniṣṭas tṛtīyaḥ // 94.62 //
||95 śākunottarādhyāyaḥ
digdeśaceṣṭāsvaravāsararkṣamuhūrtahorākaraṇodayāṃśān /
carasthironmiśrabalābalaṃ ca buddhvā phalāni pravaded rutajṇaḥ // 95.01 //
dvividhaṃ kathayanti saṃsthitānām āgāmisthirasaṃjñitaṃ ca kāryam /
nṛpadūtacarānyadeśajātāny abhighātaḥ svajanādi cāgamākhyam // 95.02 //
udbaddhasaṃgrahaṇabhojanacauravahnivarṣotsavātmajavadhāḥ kalaho bhayaṃ ca /
vargaḥ sthiro 'yam udayenduyute sthirarkṣe vidyāt sthiraṃ caragṛhe ca caraṃ yad uktam // 95.03 //
sthirapradeśopalamandireṣu surālaye bhūjalasannidhau ca /
sthirāṇi kāryāṇi carāṇi yāni calapradeśādiṣu cāgamāya // 95.04 //
āpyodayarkṣakṣaṇadigjaleṣu pakṣāvasāneṣu ca ye pradīptāḥ /
sarve 'pi te vṛṣṭikarā ruvantaḥ śānto 'pi vṛṣṭiṃ kurute 'mbucārī // 95.05 //
āgneyadiglagnamuhūrtadeśeṣv arkapradīpto 'gnibhayāya rauti /
viṣṭyāṃ yamarkṣodayakaṇṭakeṣu niṣpatravallīṣu ca doṣakṛt syāt // 95.06 //
grāmyaḥ pradīptaḥ svaraceṣṭitābhyām ugro ruvan kaṇṭakini sthitaś ca /
bhaumarkṣalagne yadi nairṛtīṃ ca sthito 'bhitaś cet kalahāya dṛṣṭaḥ // 95.07 //
lagne 'tha vendor bhṛgubhāṃśasaṃsthe vidiksthito 'dhovadanaś ca rauti /
dīptaḥ sa cet saṃgrahaṇaṃ karoti yonyā tayā yā vidiśi pradiṣṭā // 95.08 //
puṃrāśilagne viṣame tithau ca diksthaḥ pradīptaḥ śukuno narākhyaḥ /
vācyaṃ tadā saṃgrahaṇaṃ narāṇāṃ miśre bhavet paṇḍakasamprayogaḥ // 95.09 //
evaṃ raveḥ kṣetranavāṃśalagne lagne sthite vā svayam eva sūrye /
dīpto 'bhidhatte śakuno virauti puṃsaḥ pradhānasya hi kāraṇaṃ tat // 95.10 //
prārambhamāṇeṣu ca sarvakāryeṣv arkānvitād bhād gaṇayed vilagnam /
samptad vipac ceti yathā krameṇa sampad vipac ceti tathaiva vācyam // 95.11 //
kāṇenākṣṇā dakṣiṇenaiti sūrye candre lagnād dvādaśe cetarena /
lagnasthe 'rke pāpadṛṣṭe 'ndha eva kubjaḥ svarkṣe śrotrahīno jaḍo vā // 95.12 //
krūraḥ ṣaṣṭhe krūradṛṣṭo vilagnād yasmin rāśau tadgṛhāṅge vraṇo 'sya /
evaṃ proktaṃ yan mayā janmakāle cihnaṃ rūpaṃ tat tad asmin vicintyam // 95.13 //
dvyakṣaraṃ caragṛhāṃśakodaye nāma cāsya caturakṣaraṃ sthire /
nāmayugmam api ca dvimūrtiṣu tryakṣaraṃ bhavati cāsya pañcabhiḥ // 95.14 //
kādyās tu vargāḥ kujaśukrasaumyajīvārkajānāṃ kramaśaḥ pradiṣṭāḥ /
varṇāṣṭakaṃ yādi ca śītaraśme raver akārāt kramaśaḥ svarāḥ syuḥ // 95.15 //
nāmāni cāgnyambukumāraviṣṇuśakrendrapatnīcaturānanānām /
tulyāni sūryāt kramaśo vicintya dvitryādivarṇair ghaṭayet svabuddhyā // 95.16 //
vayāṃsi teṣām stanapānabālyavratasthitā yauvanamadhyavṛddhāḥ /
atīvavṛddhā iti candrabhaumajñaśukrajīvārkaśanaiścarāṇām // 95.17 //
||96 pākādhyāyaḥ
pakṣād bhānoḥ somasya māsiko 'ṅgārakasya vaktroktaḥ /
ādarśanāc ca pāko budhasya jīvasya varṣeṇa // 96.01 //
ṣaḍbhiḥ sitasya māsair abdena śaneḥ suradviṣo 'bdārdhāt /
varṣāt sūryagrahaṇe sadyaḥ syāt tvāṣṭrakīlakayoḥ // 96.02 //
tribhir eva dhūmaketor māsaiḥ śvetasya saptarātrānte /
saptāhāt pariveṣendracāpasandhyābhrasūcīnām // 96.03 //
śītoṣṇaviparyāsaḥ phalapuṣpam akālajaṃ diśāṃ dāhaḥ /
sthiracarayor anyatvaṃ prasūtivikṛtiś ca ṣaṇmāsāt // 96.04 //
akriyamāṇakakaraṇaṃ bhūkampo 'nutsavo duriṣṭaṃ ca /
śoṣaś cāśoṣyāṇāṃ sroto 'nyatvaṃ ca varṣārdhāt // 96.05 //
stambhakusūlārcānāṃ jalpitaruditaprakampitasvedāḥ /
māsatrayeṇa kalahendracāpanirghātapākāś ca // 96.06 //
kīṭākhumakṣikoragabāhulyaṃ mṛgavihaṅgavirutaṃ ca /
loṣṭasya cāpsu taraṇaṃ tribhir eva vipacyate māsaiḥ // 96.07 //
prasavaḥ śunām araṇye vanyānāṃ grāmasampraveśaś ca /
madhunilayatoraṇendradhvajāś ca varṣāt samadhikād vā // 96.08 //
gomāyugṛdhrasaṃghā daśāhikāḥ sadya eva tūryaravaḥ /
ākruṣṭaṃ pakṣaphalaṃ valmīko vidaraṇaṃ ca bhuvaḥ // 96.09 //
ahutāśaprajvalanaṃ ghṛtatailavasādivarṣaṇaṃ cāpi /
sadyaḥ paripacyante māse 'dhyardhe ca janavādaḥ // 96.10 //
chatracitiyūpahutavahabījānāṃ saptabhir bhavati pakṣaiḥ /
chatrasya toraṇasya ca kecin māsāt phalaṃ prāhuḥ // 96.11 //
atyantaviruddhānāṃ snehaḥ śabdaś ca viyati bhūtānām /
mārjāranakulayor mūṣakeṇa saṅgaś ca māsena // 96.12 //
gandharvapuraṃ māsād rasavaikṛtyaṃ hiraṇyavikṛtiś ca /
dhvajaveśmapāṃśudhūmākulā diśaś cāpi māsaphalāḥ // 96.13 //
navakaikāṣṭadaśakaikaṣaṭtrikatrikasaṅkhyamāsapākāni /
nakṣatrāṇy aśvinipūrvakāṇi sadyaḥ phalāśleṣā // 96.14 //
pitryān māsaḥ ṣaṭ saṭtrayo 'rdham aṣṭau ca triṣaḍekaikāḥ /
māsacatuṣke 'ṣāḍhe sadyaḥ pākābhijittārā // 96.15 //
saptāṣṭav adhyardhaṃ trayas trayaḥ pañca caiva māsāḥ syuḥ /
śravaṇādīnāṃ pāko nakṣatrāṇāṃ yathāsaṅkhyam // 96.16 //
nigaditasamaye na dṛśyate ced adhikataraṃ dviguṇe prapacyate tat /
yadi na kanakaratnagopradānair upaśamitaṃ vidhivad dvijaiś ca śāntyā // 96.17 //
||97 nakṣatrakarmaguṇādhyāyaḥ
śikhiguṇarasendriyānalaśaśiviṣayaguṇartupañcavasupakṣāḥ /
viṣayaikacandrabhūtārṇavāgnirudrāśvivasudahanāḥ // 97.01 //
bhūtaśatapakṣavasavo dvātriṃśac ceti tārakāmānam /
kramaśo 'śvinyādīnāṃ kālas tārāpramāṇena // 97.02 //
nakṣatrajam udvāhe phalam abdais tārakāmitaiḥ sadasat /
divasair jvarasya nāśo vyādher anyasya vā vācyaḥ // 97.03 //
aśviyamadahanakamalajaśaśiśūlabhṛdaditijīvaphaṇipitaraḥ /
yonyaryamadinakṛttvaṣṭṛpavanaśakrāgnimitrāś ca // 97.04 //
śakro nirṛtis toyaṃ viśve brahmā harir vasur varuṇaḥ /
ajapādo 'hirbudhnyaḥ pūṣā cetīśvarā bhānām // 97.05 //
trīṇy uttarāṇi tebhyo rohiṇyaś ca dhruvāṇi taiḥ kuryāt /
abhiṣekaśāntitarunagaradharmabījadhruvārambhān // 97.06 //
mūlaśivaśakrabhujagādhipāni tīkṣṇāni teṣu siddhyanti /
abhighātamantravetālabandhavadhabhedasaṃbandhāḥ // 97.07 //
ugrāṇi pūrvabharaṇīpitryāṇy utsādanāśaśāṭhyeṣu /
yojyāni bandhaviṣadahanaśastraghātādiṣu ca siddhyai // 97.08 //
laghu hastāśvinapuṣyāḥ paṇyaratijñānabhūṣaṇakalāsu /
śilpauṣadhayānādiṣu siddhikarāṇi pradiṣṭāni // 97.09 //
mṛduvargo 'nūrādhācitrāpauṣṇaindavāni mitrārthe /
suratavidhivastrabhūṣaṇamaṅgalagīteṣu ca hitāni // 97.10 //
hautabhujaṃ saviśākhaṃ mṛdutīkṣṇam tadvimiśraphalakāri /
śravaṇatrayam ādityānile ca carakarmaṇi hitāni // 97.11 //
hastatrayaṃ mṛgaśiraḥ śravaṇatrayaṃ ca pūṣāśviśakragurubhāni punarvasuś ca /
kṣaure tu karmaṇi hitāny udaye kṣaṇe vā yuktāni coḍupatinā śubhatārayā ca // 97.12 //
na snātamātragamanonmukhabhūṣitānām abhyaktabhuktaraṇakālanirāsanānām /
sandhyāniśāśanikujārkatithau ca rikte kṣauraṃ hitaṃ na navame 'hni na cāpi viṣṭyām // 97.13 //
nṛpājñayā brāhmaṇasammate ca vivāhakāle mṛtasūtake ca /
baddhasya mokṣe kratudīkṣaṇāsu sarveṣu śastaṃ kṣurakarma bheṣu // 97.14 //
sāvitrapauṣṇānilamaitratiṣyatvāṣṭre tathā coḍugaṇādhiparkṣe /
saṃskāradīkṣāvratamekhalādi kuryād gurau śukrabudhenduyukte // 97.15 //
śuddhair dvādaśakendranaidhanagṛhaiḥ pāpais triṣaṣṭhāyagair lagne kendragate 'tha vā suragurau daityendrapūjye 'pi vā /
sarvārambhaphalaprasiddhir udaye rāśau ca kartuḥ śubhe sagrāmyasthirabhodaye ca bhavanaṃ kāryaṃ praveśo 'pi vā // 97.16 //
||98 tithikarmaguṇādhyāyaḥ
kamalajavidhātṛhariyamaśaśāṅkaṣaḍvaktraśakravasubhujagāḥ /
dharmeśasavitṛmanmathakalayo viśve ca tithipatayaḥ // 98.01 //
pitaro 'māvasyāyāṃ saṃjñāsadṛśāśca taiḥ kriyāḥ kāryāḥ /
nandā bhadrā vijayā riktā pūrṇā ca tās trividhāḥ // 98.02 //
yat kāryaṃ nakṣatre taddaivatyāsu tithiṣu tat kāryam /
karaṇamuhūrteṣv api tat siddhikaraṃ devatāsadṛśam // 98.03 //
||99 karaṇaguṇādhyāyaḥ
vavavālavakaulavataitilākhyagaravaṇijaviṣṭisaṃjñānām /
patayaḥ syur indrakamalajamitrāryamabhūśriyaḥ sayamāḥ // 99.01 //
kṛṣṇacaturdaśyardhād dhuvāṇi śakuniś catuṣpadaṃ nāgam /
kiṃstughnam iti ca teṣāṃ kalivṛṣaphaṇimārutāḥ patayaḥ // 99.02 //
kuryād vave śubhacarasthirapauṣṭikāni dharmakriyādvijahitāni ca vālavākhye /
samprītimitravaraṇāni ca kaulave syuḥ saubhāgyasaṃśrayagṛhāṇi ca taitilākhye // 99.03 //
kṛṣibījagṛhāśrayajāni gare vaṇiji dhuvakāryavaṇigyutayaḥ /
na hi viṣṭikṛtaṃ vidadhāti śubhaṃ paraghātaviṣādiṣu siddhikaram // 99.04 //
kāryaṃ pauṣṭikam auṣadhādi śakunau mūlāni mantrās tathā gokāryāṇi catuṣpade dvijapitṛn uddiśya rājyāni ca /
nāge sthāvaradāruṇāni haraṇaṃ daurbhāgyakarmāṇy ataḥ kiṃstughne śubham iṣṭipuṣṭikaraṇaṃ maṅgalyasiddhikriyāḥ // 99.05 //
lābhe tṛtīye ca śubhaiḥ samete pāpair vihīne śubharāśilagne /
vedhyau ca karṇāv amarejyalagne puṣyenducitrāharipauṣṇabheṣu // 99.06 //
rohiṇyuttararevatīmṛgaśiromūlānurādhāmaghāhastasvātiṣu ṣaṣṭhataulimithuneṣūdyatsu pāṇigrahaḥ /
saptāṣṭāntyabahiḥśubhair uḍupatāv ekādaśadvitrige krūrais tryāyaṣaḍaṣṭagair na tu bhṛgau ṣaṣṭhe kuje cāṣṭame // 99.07 //
dampatyor dvinavāṣṭarāśirahite cārānukule ravau candre cārkakujārkiśukraviyute madhye 'tha vā pāpayoḥ /
tyaktvā ca vyatipātavaidhṛtidinaṃ viṣṭiṃ ca riktāṃ tithiṃ krūrāhāyanapauṣacaitravirahe lagnāṃśake mānuṣe // 99.08 //
||100 nakṣatrajātakādhyāyaḥ
priyabhūṣaṇaḥ svarūpaḥ subhago dakṣo 'śvinīṣu matimāṃś ca /
kṛtaniścayasatyārugdakṣaḥ sukhitaś ca bharaṇīṣu // 100.01 //
bahubhuk paradāraratas tejasvī kṛttikāsu vikhyātaḥ /
rohiṇyāṃ satyaśuciḥ priyaṃvadaḥ sthiraḥ svarūpaś ca // 100.02 //
capalaś caturo bhīruḥ paṭur utsāhī dhanī mṛge bhogī /
śaṭhagarvitacaṇḍakṛtaghnahiṃsrapāpaś ca raudrarkṣe // 100.03 //
dāntaḥ sukhī suśīlo durmedhā rogabhāk pipāsuś ca /
alpena ca santuṣṭaḥ punarvasau jāyate manujaḥ // 100.04 //
śāntātmā subhagaḥ paṇḍito dhanī dharmasaṃśritaḥ puṣye /
śaṭhasarvabhakṣakṣyapāpaḥ kṛtaghnadhūrtaś ca bhaujaṅge // 100.05 //
bahubhṛtyadhanī bhogī surapitṛbhakto mahodyamaḥ pitrye /
priyavāg dātā dyutimān aṭano nṛpasevako bhāgye // 100.06 //
subhago vidyāptadhano bhogī sukhabhāg dvitīyaphalgunyām /
utsāhī dhṛṣṭaḥ pānapo 'ghṛṇī taskaro haste // 100.07 //
citrāmbaramālyadharaḥ sulocanāṅgaś ca citrāyām /
dānto vaṇik tṛṣāluḥ priyavāg dharmāśritaḥ svātau // 100.08 //
īrṣur lubdho dyutimān vacanapaṭuḥ kalahakṛd viśākhāsu // 100.09 //
āḍhyo videśavāsī kṣudhālur aṭano 'nurādhāsu // 100.09 //
jyeṣṭhāsu na bahumitraḥ santuṣṭo dharmakṛt pracurakopaḥ /
mūle mānī dhanavān sukhī na hiṃsraḥ sthiro bhogī // 100.10 //
iṣṭānandakalatro vīro dṛḍhasauhṛdaś ca jaladeve /
vaiśve vinītadhārmikabahumitrakṛtajñasubhagaś ca // 100.11 //
śrīmān śravaṇe śrutavān udāradāro dhanānvitaḥ khyātaḥ /
dātāḍhyaśūragītapriyo dhaniṣṭhāsu dhanalubdhaḥ // 100.12 //
sphuṭavāg vyasanī ripuhā sāhasikaḥ śatabhiṣaksu durgrāhyaḥ /
bhadrapadāsūdvignaḥ strījitadhanapaṭur adātā ca // 100.13 //
vaktā sukhī prajāvān jitaśatrur dhārmiko dvitīyāsu // 100.14 //
sampūrṇāṅgaḥ subhagaḥ śūraḥ śucir arthavān pauṣṇe // 100.14 //
||101 rāśivibhāgādhyāyaḥ
aśvinyo 'tha bharaṇyo bahulāpādaś ca kīrtyate meṣaḥ /
vṛṣabho bahulāśeṣaṃ rohiṇyo 'rdham ca mṛgaśirasaḥ // 101.01 //
mṛgaśiro 'rdhaṃ raudraṃ punarvasor aṃśakatrayaṃ mithunaḥ /
pādaś ca punarvasutas tiṣyaḥ śleṣā ca karkaṭakaḥ // 101.02 //
siṃho 'tha maghā pūrvā ca phalgunī pāda uttarāyāś ca /
tatpariśeṣaṃ hastaś citrādyardhaṃ ca kanyākhyaḥ // 101.03 //
taulini citrāntyārdhaṃ svātiḥ pādatrayaṃ viśākhāyāḥ /
alini viśākhāpādas tathānurādhānvitā jyeṣṭhā // 101.04 //
mūlam aṣāḍhā pūrvā prathamaś cāpy uttarāṃśako dhanvī /
makaras tatpariṣeśaṃ śravaṇaḥ pūrvaṃ dhaniṣṭhārdham // 101.05 //
kumbho 'ntyadhaniṣṭhārdhaṃ śatabhiṣagaṃśatrayaṃ ca pūrvāyāḥ /
bhadrapadāyāḥ śeṣaṃ tathottarā revatī ca jhaṣaḥ // 101.06 //
aśvinīpitryamūlādyā meṣasiṃhahayādayaḥ /
viṣamarkṣān nivartante pādavṛddhyā yathottaram // 101.07 //
||102 vivāhapaṭalādhyāyaḥ
mūrtau karoti dinakṛd vidhavāṃ kujaś ca rāhur vipannatanayāṃ ravijo daridrām /
śukraḥ śaśāṅkatanayaś ca guruś ca sādhvīm āyuḥkṣayaṃ prakurute 'tha vibhāvarīśaḥ // 102.01 //
kurvanti bhāskaraśanaiścararāhubhaumā dāridryaduḥkham atulaṃ niyataṃ dvitīye /
vitteśvarīm avidhavāṃ guruśukrasaumyā nārīṃ prabhūtatanayāṃ kurute śaśāṅkaḥ // 102.02 //
sūryendubhaumaguruśukrabudhās tṛtīye kuryuḥ sadā bahusutāṃ dhanabhāginīṃ ca /
vyaktāṃ divākarasutaḥ subhagāṃ karoti mṛtyuṃ dadāti niyamāt khalu saiṃhikeyaḥ // 102.03 //
svalpaṃ payaḥ sravati sūryasute caturthe daurbhāgyam uṣṇakiraṇaḥ kurute śaśī ca /
rāhuḥ sapatnanam api ca kṣitijo 'lpavittaṃ dadyād bhṛguḥ suraguruś ca budhaś ca saukhyam // 102.04 //
naṣṭātmajāṃ ravikujau khalu pañcamasthe candrātmajo bahusutā gurubhārgavau ca /
rāhur dadāti maraṇaṃ śanir ugrarogaṃ kanyāvināśam acirāt kurute śaśāṅkaḥ // 102.05 //
ṣaṣṭhāśritāḥ śanidivākararāhujīvāḥ kuryuḥ kujaś ca subhagāṃ śvaśureṣu bhaktām /
candraḥ karoti vidhavām uśanā daridrām ṛddhāṃ śaśāṅkatanayaḥ kalahapriyāṃ ca // 102.06 //
saurārajīvabudharāhuravīnduśukrāḥ kuryuḥ prasahya khalu saptamarāśisaṃsthāḥ /
vaidhavyabandhanavadhakṣayam arthanāśavyādhipravāsamaraṇāni yathākrameṇa // 102.07 //
sthāne 'ṣṭame gurubudhau niyataṃ viyogaṃ mṛtyuṃ śaśī bhṛgusutaś ca tathaiva rāhuḥ /
sūryaḥ karoty avidhavāṃ sarujāṃ mahījaḥ sūryātmajo dhanavatīṃ pativallabhāṃ ca // 102.08 //
dharme sthitā bhṛgudivākarabhūmiputrā jīvaś ca dharmaniratāṃ śaśijas tv arogām /
rāhuś ca sūryatanayaś ca karoti bandhyāṃ kanyāprasūtim aṭanāṃ kurute śaśāṅkaḥ // 102.09 //
rāhur nabhaḥsthalagato vidhavāṃ karoti pāpe ratāṃ dinakaraś ca śanaiścaraś ca /
mṛtyuṃ kujo 'rtharahitāṃ kulaṭāṃ ca candraḥ śeṣā grahā dhanavatīṃ subhagāṃ ca kuryuḥ // 102.10 //
āye ravir bahusutāṃ sadhanāṃ śaśāṅkaḥ putrānvitāṃ kṣitisuto ravijo dhanāḍhyām /
āyuṣmatīṃ suraguruḥ śaśijaḥ samṛddhāṃ rāhuḥ karoty avidhavāṃ bhṛgur arthayuktām // 102.11 //
ante gurur dhanavatīṃ dinakṛd daridrāṃ candro dhanavyayakarīṃ kulaṭāṃ ca rāhuḥ /
sādhvīṃ bhṛguḥ śaśisuto bahuputrapautrāṃ pānaprasaktahṛdayām ravijaḥ kujaś ca // 102.12 //
gopair yaṣṭyāhatānāṃ khurapuṭadalitā yā tu dhūlir dinānte sodvāhe sundarīṇāṃ vipuladhanasutārogyasaubhāgyakartrī /
tasmin kāle na carkṣaṃ na ca tithikaraṇaṃ naiva lagnaṃ na yogaḥ khyātaḥ puṃsāṃ sukhārthaṃ śamayati duritāny utthitaṃ gorajas tu // 102.13 //
||103 grahagocarādhyāyaḥ
prāyeṇa sūtreṇa vinākṛtāni prakāśarandhrāṇi cirantanāni /
ratnāni śāstrāṇi ca yojitāni navair guṇair bhūṣayituṃ kṣamāṇi // 103.01 //
prāyeṇa gocaro vyavahāryo 'tas tatphalāni vakṣyāmi /
nānāvṛttair āryā mukhacapalatvaṃ kṣamadhvaṃ naḥ // 103.02 //
māṇḍavyagiraṃ śrutvā na madīyā rocate 'tha vā naivam /
sādhvī tathā na puṃsāṃ priyā yathā syāj jaghanacapalā // 103.03 //
sūryaḥ ṣaṭtridaśasthitas tridaśaṣaṭsaptādyagaś candramā jīvaḥ saptanavadvipañcamagato vakrārkajau ṣaṭtrigau /
saumyaḥ ṣaḍdvicaturdaśāṣṭamagataḥ sūrye 'py upānte śubhāḥ śukraḥ saptamaṣaḍdaśarkṣasahitaḥ śārdūlavat trāsakṛt // 103.04 //
janmany āyāsado 'rkaḥ kṣapayati vibhavān koṣṭharogādhvadātā vittabhraṃśaṃ dvitīye diśati ca na sukhaṃ vañcanāṃ dṛgrujaṃ ca /
sthānaprāptiṃ tṛtīye dhananicayamudā kalyakṛc cārihartā rogān datte caturthe janayati ca muhuḥ sragdharābhogavighnam // 103.05 //
pīḍāḥ syuḥ pañcamasthe savitari bahuśo rogārijanitāḥ ṣaṣṭhe 'rko hanti rogān kṣapayati ca ripūn śokāṃś ca nudati /
adhvānaṃ saptamastho jaṭharagadabhayaṃ dainyaṃ ca kurute /
ruktrāsau cāṣṭamasthe bhavati suvadanā na svāpi vanitā // 103.06 //
ravāv āpaddainyaṃ rug iti navame vittaceṣṭāvirodho jayaṃ prāpnoty ugraṃ daśamagṛhage karmasiddhiṃ krameṇa /
jayasthānaṃ mānaṃ vibhavam api caikādaśe roganāśaṃ suvṛttānāṃ ceṣṭā bhavati saphalā dvādaśe netareṣām // 103.07 //
śaśī janmany annapravaraśayanācchādanakaro dvitīye mānārthān glapayati savighnaś ca bhavati /
tṛtīye vastrastrīdhanavijayasaukhyāni labhate caturthe 'viśvāsaḥ śikhariṇi bhujaṅgena sadṛśaḥ // 103.08 //
dainyaṃ vyādhiṃ śucam api śaśī pañcame mārgavighnaṃ ṣaṣṭhe vittaṃ janayati sukhaṃ śatrurogakṣayaṃ ca /
yānaṃ mānaṃ śayanam aśanaṃ saptame vittalābhaṃ mandākrānte phaṇini himagau ca aṣṭame bhīr na kasya // 103.09 //
navamagṛhago bandhodvegaśramodararogakṛd daśamabhavane ca ājñākarmaprasiddhikaraḥ śaśī /
upacayasuhṛtsaṃyogārthapramodam upāntyago vṛṣabhacaritān doṣān antye karoti ca savyayān // 103.10 //
kuje 'bhighātaḥ prathame dvitīye narendrapīḍā kalahāridoṣaiḥ /
bhṛśaṃ ca pittānalacaurarogair upendravajrapratimo 'pi yaḥ syāt // 103.11 //
tṛtīyagaś caurakumārakebhyo bhaumaḥ sakāśāt phalam ādadhāti /
pradīptim ājñāṃ dhanam aurṇikāni dhātvākarākhyāni kila aparāṇi // 103.12 //
bhavati dharaṇije caturthage jvarajaṭharagadāsṛgudbhavaḥ /
kupuruṣajanitāc ca saṅgamāt prasabham api karoti ca aśubham // 103.13 //
ripugadakopabhayāni pañcame tanayakṛtāś ca śuco mahīsute /
dyutir api na asya ciraṃ bhavet sthirā śirasi kaper iva mālatī yathā // 103.14 //
ripubhayakalahair vivarjitaḥ sakanakavidrumatāmrakāmagaḥ /
ripubhavanagate mahīsute kim aparavaktravikāram īkṣate // 103.15 //
kalatrakalahākṣirugjaṭhararogakṛt saptame kṣaratkṣatajarūkṣitaḥ kṣapitavittamāno 'ṣṭame /
kuje navamasaṃsthite paribhavārthanāśādibhir vilambitagatir bhavaty abaladehadhātuklamaiḥ // 103.16 //
daśamagṛhagate samaṃ mahīje vividhadhanāptir upāntyage jayaś ca /
janapadam upari sthitaś ca bhuṅkte vanam iva ṣaṭcaraṇaḥ supuṣpitāgram // 103.17 //
nānāvyayair dvādaśage mahīsute santāpyate 'narthaśataiś ca mānavaḥ /
strīkopapittaiś ca sanetravedanair yo 'pi indravaṃśābhijanena garvitaḥ // 103.18 //
duṣṭavākyapiśunāhitabhedair bandhanaiḥ sakalahaiś ca hṛtasvaḥ /
janmage śaśisute pathi gacchan svāgate 'pi kuśalaṃ na śṛṇoti // 103.19 //
paribhavo dhanagate dhanalabdhiḥ sahajage śaśisute hṛdayāptiḥ /
nṛpatiśatrubhayaśaṅkitacito drutapadaṃ vrajati duścaritaiḥ svaiḥ // 103.20 //
caturthage svajanakuṭumbavṛddhayo dhanāgamo bhavati ca śītaraśmije /
sutasthite tanayakalatravigraho niṣevate na ca rucirām api striyam // 103.21 //
saubhāgyaṃ vijayam atha unnatiṃ ca ṣaṣṭhe vaivarṇyaṃ kalaham atīva saptame jñaḥ /
mṛtyusthe jayasutavastravittalābhā naipuṇyaṃ bhavati matipraharṣaṇīyam // 103.22 //
vighnakaro navamaḥ śaśiputraḥ karmagato ripuhā dhanadaś ca /
sapramadaṃ śayanaṃ ca vidhatte tadgṛhado 'tha kathāṃ staraṇaṃ ca // 103.23 //
dhanasutasukhayoṣinmitravāhāptituṣṭis tuhinakiraṇaputre lābhage mṛṣṭavākyaḥ /
ripuparibhavarogaiḥ pīḍito dvādaśasthe na sahati paribhoktuṃ mālinīyogasaukhyam // 103.24 //
jīve janmany apagatadhanadhīḥ sthānabhraṣṭo bahukalahayutaḥ /
prāpya arthe 'rthān vyarir api kurute kāntāsyābje bhramaravilasitam // 103.25 //
sthānabhraṃśāt kāryavighātāc ca tṛtīye 'nekaiḥ kleśair bandhujanotthaiś ca caturthe /
jīve śāntiṃ pīḍitacittaś ca sa vinded naiva grāme nāpi vane mattamayūre // 103.26 //
janayati ca tanayabhavanam upagataḥ parijanaśubhasutakarituragavṛṣān /
sakanakapuragṛhayuvativasanakṛn maṇiguṇanikarakṛd api vibudhaguruḥ // 103.27 //
na sakhīvadanaṃ tilakojjvalaṃ na ca vanaṃ śikhikokilanāditam /
hariṇaplutaśāvavicitritaṃ ripugate manasaḥ sukhadaṃ gurau // 103.28 //
tridaśaguruḥ śayanaṃ ratibhogaṃ dhanam aśanaṃ kusumāny upavāhyam /
janayati saptamarāśim upeto lalitapadāṃ ca giraṃ dhiṣaṇāṃ ca // 103.29 //
bandhaṃ vyādhim cāṣṭame śokam ugraṃ mārgakleśān mṛtyutulyāṃś ca rogān /
naipuṇyājñāputrakarmārthasiddhiṃ dharme jīvaḥ śālinīnāṃ ca lābham // 103.30 //
sthānakalyadhanahā daśarkṣagas tatprado bhavati lābhago guruḥ /
dvādaśe 'dhvani vilomaduḥkhabhāg yāti yady api naro rathoddhataḥ // 103.31 //
prathamagṛhopago bhṛgusutaḥ smaropakaraṇaiḥ surabhimanojñagandhakusumāmbarair upacayam /
śayanagṛhāsanāśanayutasya ca anukurute samadavilāsinīmukhasarojaṣaṭcaraṇatām // 103.32 //
śukre dvitīyagṛhage prasavārthadhānyabhūpālasannatakuṭumbahitāny avāpya /
saṃsevate kusumaratnavibhūṣitaś ca kāmaṃ vasantatilakadyutimūrdhajo 'pi // 103.33 //
ājñārthamānāspadabhūtivastraśatrukṣayān daityagurus tṛtīye /
datte caturthaś ca suhṛtsamājaṃ rudrendravajrapratimāṃ ca śaktim // 103.34 //
janayati śukraḥ pañcamasaṃstho guruparitoṣaṃ bandhujanāptim /
sutadhanalabdhiṃ mitrasahāyān anavasitatvaṃ ca aribaleṣu // 103.35 //
ṣaṣṭho bhṛguḥ paribhavarogatāpadaḥ strīhetukaṃ janayati saptamo 'śubham /
yāto 'ṣṭamaṃ bhavanaparicchadaprado lakṣmīvatīm upanayati striyaṃ ca saḥ // 103.36 //
navame tu dharmavanitāsukhabhāg bhṛguje 'rthavastranicayaś ca bhavet /
daśame 'vamānakalahān niyamāt pramitākṣarāṇy api vadan labhate // 103.37 //
upāntyago bhṛgo sutaḥ suhṛddhanānnagandhadaḥ /
dhanāmbarāgamo 'ntyagaḥ sthiras tu nāmbarāgamaḥ // 103.38 //
prathame ravije viṣavahnihataḥ svajanair viyutaḥ kṛtabandhuvadhaḥ /
paradeśam upaity asuhṛdbhavano vimukhārthasuto 'ṭakadīnamukhaḥ // 103.39 //
cāravaśād dvitīyagṛhage dinakaratanaye rūpasukhāpavarjitatanur vigatamadabalaḥ /
anyaguṇaiḥ kṛtaṃ vasucayam tad api khalu bhavaty ambv iva vaṃśapatrapatitaṃ na bahu na ca ciram // 103.40 //
sūryasute tṛtīyagṛhage dhanāni labhate dāsaparicchadoṣṭramahiṣāśvakuñjarakharān /
sadmavibhūtisaukhyam amitaṃ gadavyuparamaṃ bhīrur api praśāsty adhiripūṃś ca vīralalitaiḥ // 103.41 //
caturthaṃ gṛhaṃ sūryaputre 'bhyupete suhṛdvittabhāryādibhir viprayuktaḥ /
bhavaty asya sarvatra cāsādhu duṣṭaṃ bhujaṅgaprayātānukāraṃ ca cittam // 103.42 //
sutadhanaparihīṇaḥ pañcamasthe pracurakalahayuktaś ca arkaputre /
vinihataripurogaḥ ṣaṣṭhayāte pibati ca vanitāsyaṃ śrīpuṭoṣṭham // 103.43 //
gacchaty adhvānaṃ saptame ca aṣṭame ca hīnaḥ strīputraiḥ sūryaje dīnaceṣṭaḥ /
tadvad dharmasthe vairahṛdrogabandhair dharmo 'py ucchidyed vaiśvadevīkriyādyaḥ // 103.44 //
karmaprāptir daśame 'rthakṣayaś ca vidyākīrtyoḥ parihāniś ca saure /
taikṣṇyaṃ lābhe parayoṣārthalābhaś ca antye prāpnoty api śokormimālām // 103.45 //
api kālam apekṣya ca pātraṃ śubhakṛd vidadhāty anurūpam /
na madhau bahu kaṃ kuḍave vā visṛjaty api meghavitānaḥ // 103.46 //
raktaiḥ puṣpair gandhais tāmraiḥ kanakavṛṣabakulakusumair divākarabhūsutau bhaktyā pūjyāv indur dhenvā sitakusumarajatamadhuraiḥ sitaś ca madapradaiḥ /
kṛṣṇadravyaiḥ sauriḥ saumyo maṇirajatatilakakusumair guruḥ paripītakaiḥ prītaiḥ pīḍā na syād uccād yadi patati viśati yadi vā bhujaṅgavijṛmbhitam // 103.47 //
śamayodgatām aśubhadṛṣṭim api vibudhaviprapūjayā /
śāntijapaniyamadānadamaiḥ sujanābhibhāṣaṇasamāgamais tathā // 103.48 //
ravibhaumau pūrvārdhe śaśisaurau kathayato 'ntyagau rāśeḥ /
sadasallakṣaṇam āryagītyupagītyor yathāsaṃkhyam // 103.49 //
ādau yādṛk saumyaḥ paścād api tādṛśo bhavati /
upagīter mātrāṇāṃ gaṇavat satsamprayogo vā // 103.50 //
āryāṇām api kurute vināśam antargurur viṣamasaṃsthaḥ /
gaṇa iva ṣaṣṭhe dṛṣṭaḥ sa sarvalaghutāṃ janaṃ nayati // 103.51 //
aśubhanirīkṣitaḥ śubhaphalo balinā balavān aśubhaphalapradaś ca śubhadṛgviṣayopagataḥ /
aśubhaśubhāv api svaphalayor vrajataḥ samatām idam api gītakaṃ ca khalu narkuṭakaṃ ca yathā // 103.52 //
nīce 'ribhe 'ste ca aridṛṣṭasya sarvaṃ vṛthā yat parikīrtitam /
purato 'ndhasya iva kāminyāḥ savilāsakaṭākṣanirīkṣaṇam // 103.53 //
sūryasuto 'rkaphalasamaś candrasutaś chandataḥ samanuyāti yathā /
skandhakam āryāgītir vaitālīyaṃ ca māgadhī gāthāryām // 103.54 //
sauro 'rkaraśmiyogāt savikāro labdhavṛddhir adhikataram /
pittavad ācarati nṛṇāṃ pathyakṛtāṃ na tu tathāryāṇām // 103.55 //
yādṛśena graheṇendur yuktas tādṛg bhavet so 'pi /
manovṛttisamāyogād vikāra iva vaktrasya // 103.56 //
pañcamaṃ laghu sarveṣu saptamaṃ dvicaturthayoḥ /
yadvacchlokākṣaraṃ tadval laghutāṃ yāti duḥsthitaiḥ // 103.57 //
prakṛtyāpi laghur yaś ca vṛttabāhye vyavasthitaḥ /
sa yāti gurutāṃ loke yadā syuḥ susthitā grahāḥ // 103.58 //
prārabdham asusthitair grahair yat karmātmavivṛddhaye budhaiḥ /
vinihanti tad eva karma tān vaitālīyam iva ayathākṛtam // 103.59 //
sausthityam avekṣya yo grahebhyaḥ kāle prakramaṇaṃ karoti rājā /
aṇunā api sa pauruṣeṇa vṛttasyaupacchandasikasya yāti pāram // 103.60 //
upacayabhavanopayātasya bhānor dine kārayed dhematāmrāśvakāṣṭhāsthicarmaurṇikādridrumatvaṅnakhavyālacaurāyudhīyāṭavīkrūrarājopasevābhiṣekauṣadhakṣaumapaṇyādigopālakāntāravaidyāśmakūṭāvadātābhivikhyātaśūrāhavaślāghyayāyyagnikarmāṇi siddhyanti lagnasthite vā ravau /
śiśirakiraṇavāsare tasya va apy udgame kendrasaṃsthe 'tha vā bhūṣaṇaṃ śaṅkhamuktābjarūpyāmbuyajñekṣubhojyāṅganākṣīrasusnigdhavṛkṣakṣupānūpadhānyadravadravyaviprādhvagītakriyāśṛṅgikṛṣyādisenādhipākrandabhūpālasaubhāgyanaktañcaraślaiṣmikadravyamātulyapuṣpāmbarārambhasiddhir bhavet /
kṣititanayadine prasiddhyanti dhātvākarādīni sarvāṇi kāryāṇi cāmīkarāgnipravālāyudhakrauryacauryābhighātāṭavīdurgasenādhikārās tathā raktapuṣpadrumā raktam anyac ca tiktaṃ kaṭudravyakūṭāhipāśārjitasvāḥ kumārā bhiṣakśākyabhikṣukṣapāvṛttikośeśaśāṭhyāni siddhyanti dambhās tathā /
haratimaṇimahīsugandhīni vastrāṇi sādhāraṇaṃ nāṭakaṃ śāstravijñānakāvyāni sarvāḥ kalāyuktayo mantradhātukriyāvādanaipuṇyapuṇyavratāyogadūtās tathāyuṣyamāyānṛtasnānahrasvāṇi dīrghāṇi madhyāni ca chandataś caṇḍavṛṣṭiprayātānukārīṇi kāryāṇi siddhyanti saumyasya lagne 'hni vā // 103.61 //
suragurudivase kanakaṃ rajataṃ turagāḥ kariṇo vṛṣabhā bhiṣagauṣadhayaḥ dvijapitṛsurakāryapuraḥsthitagharmanivāraṇacāmarabhūṣaṇabhūpatayaḥ /
vibudhabhavanadharmasamāśrayamaṅgalaśāstramanojñabalapradasatyagiraḥ vratahavanadhanāni ca siddhikarāṇi tathā rucirāṇi ca varṇakadaṇḍakavat // 103.62 //
bhṛgusutadivase ca citravastravṛṣyaveśyakāminīvilāsahāsayauvanopabhogaramyabhūmayaḥ sphaṭikarajatamanmathopacāravāhanekṣuśāradaprakāragovaṇikkṛṣīvalauṣadhāmbujāni ca /
savitṛsutadine ca kārayen mahiṣyajoṣṭrakṛṣṇalohadāsavṛddhanīcakarmapakṣicaurapāśikān cyutavinayaviśīrṇabhāṇḍahastyapekṣavighnakāraṇāni ca anyathā na sādhayet samudrago 'py apāṃ kaṇam // 103.63 //
vipulām api buddhvā chandovicitiṃ bhavati kāryam etāvat /
śrutisukhadavṛttasaṃgraham imam āha varāhamihiro 'taḥ // 103.64 //
||104 rūpasatrādhyāyaḥ
pādau mūlaṃ jaṅghe ca rohiṇī jānunī tathāśvinyaḥ /
ūrū ca āṣāḍhadvayam atha guhyaṃ phalgunīdvitayam // 104.01 //
kaṭir api ca kṛttikā pārśvayoś ca yamalā bhavanti bhadrapadāḥ /
kukṣisthā revatyo vijñeyam uro 'nurādhā ca // 104.02 //
pṛṣṭhaṃ viddhi dhaniṣṭhāṃ bhujau viśākhā smṛtau karau hastaḥ // 104.03 //
aṅgulyaś ca punarvasur āśleṣāsaṃjñitāś ca nakhāḥ // 104.03 //
grīvā jyeṣṭhā śravaṇaṃ śravaṇau puṣyo mukhaṃ dvijāḥ svātiḥ /
hasitaṃ śatabhiṣag atha nāsikā maghā mṛgaśiro netre // 104.04 //
citrā lalāṭasaṃsthā śiro bharaṇyaḥ śiroruhāś cārdrā /
nakṣatrapuruṣako 'yaṃ kartavyo rūpam icchadbhiḥ // 104.05 //
caitrasya bahulapakṣe hy aṣṭamyāṃ mūlasaṃyute candre /
hy upavāsaḥ kartavyo viṣṇuṃ sampūjya dhiṣṇyaṃ ca // 104.06 //
dadyād vrate samāpte ghṛtapūrṇaṃ bhājanaṃ suvarṇayutam /
viprāya kālaviduṣe saratnavastraṃ svaśaktyā ca // 104.07 //
annaiḥ kṣīraghṛtotkaṭaiḥ saha guḍair viprān samabhyarcayed dadyāt teṣu suvarṇavastrarajataṃ lāvaṇyam icchan naraḥ /
pādarkṣāt prabhṛti kramād upavasann aṅgarkṣanāmasv api kuryāt keśavapūjanaṃ svavidhinā dhiṣṇyasya pūjāṃ tathā // 104.08 //
pralambabāhuḥ pṛthupīnavakṣāḥ kṣapākarāsyaḥ sitacārudantaḥ /
gajendragāmī kamalāyatākṣaḥ strīcittahārī smaratulyamūrtiḥ // 104.09 //
śaradamalapūrṇacandradyutisadṛśamukhī sarojadalanetrā /
ruciradaśanā sukarṇā bhramarodarasannibhaiḥ keśaiḥ // 104.10 //
puṃskokilasamavāṇī tāmroṣṭī padmapatrakaracaraṇā /
stanabhārānatamadhyā pradakṣiṇāvartayā nābhyā // 104.11 //
kadalīkāṇḍanibhoruḥ suśroṇī varakukundarā subhagā /
suśliṣṭāṅgulipādā bhavati pramadā manuṣyaś ca // 104.12 //
yāvan nakṣatramālā vicarati gagane bhūṣayantī iha bhāsā tāvan nakṣatrabhūto vicarati saha tair brahmaṇo 'hno 'vaśeṣam /
kalpādau cakravartī bhavati hi matimāṃs tatkṣayāc cāpi bhūyaḥ saṃsāre jāyamāno bhavati narapatir brāhmaṇo vā dhanāḍhyaḥ // 104.13 //
mṛgaśīrṣādyāḥ keśavanārāyaṇamādhavāḥ sagovindāḥ /
viṣṇumadhusūdanākhyau trivikramo vāmanaś caiva // 104.14 //
śrīdharanāmā tasmāt sahṛṣīkeśaś ca padmanābhaś ca /
dāmodara ity ete māsāḥ proktā yathāsaṃkhyaṃ //
māsanāma samupoṣito naro dvādaśīṣu vidhivat prakīrtayan /
keśavam samabhipūjya tatpadaṃ yāti yatra nahi janmajaṃ bhayam // 104.16 //
||105 upasaṃhārādhyāyaḥ
jyotiḥśāstrasamudraṃ pramathya matimandarādriṇātha mayā /
lokasya ālokakaraḥ śāstraśaśāṅkaḥ samutkṣiptaḥ // 105.01 //
pūrvācāryagranthā notsṛṣṭāḥ kurvatā mayā śāstram /
tān avalokyedaṃ ca prayatadhvaṃ kāmataḥ sujanāḥ // 105.02 //
atha vā kṛśam api sujanaḥ prathayati doṣārṇavād guṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā /
nīcas tadviparītaḥ prakṛtir iyaṃ sādhvasādhūnām // 105.03 //
durjanahutāśataptaṃ kāvyasuvarṇaṃ viśuddhim āyāti /
śrāvayitavyaṃ tasmād duṣṭajanasya prayatnena // 105.04 //
granthasya yat pracarato 'sya vināśam eti lekhyād bahuśrutamukhādhigamakrameṇa /
yadvā mayā kukṛtam alpam ihākṛtaṃ vā kāryaṃ tad atra viduṣā parihṛtya rāgam // 105.05 //
dinakaramunigurucaraṇapraṇipātakṛtaprasādamatinedam /
śāstram upasaṅgṛhītaṃ namo 'stu pūrvapraṇetṛbhyaḥ // 105.06 //
||106 śāstrānukramaṇī
śāstropanayaḥ pūrvaṃ sāṃvatsarasūtram arkacāraś ca /
śaśirāhubhaumabudhagurusitamandaśikhigrahāṇāṃ ca // 106.01 //
cāraś cāgastyamuneḥ saptarṣīṇāṃ ca kūrmayogaś ca /
nakṣatrāṇāṃ vyūho grahabhaktir grahavimardaś ca // 106.02 //
grahaśaśiyogaḥ samyaggrahavarṣaphalaṃ grahāṇāṃ ca /
śṛṅgāṭasaṃsthitānāṃ meghānāṃ garbhalakṣaṇaṃ caiva // 106.03 //
dhāraṇavarṣaṇarohiṇivāyavyāṣāḍhabhadrapadayogāḥ /
kṣaṇavṛṣṭiḥ kusumalatāḥ sandhyācihnaṃ diśāṃ dāhaḥ // 106.04 //
bhūkampolkāpariveṣalakṣaṇaṃ śakracāpakhapuraṃ ca /
pratisūryo nirghātaḥ sasyadravyārghakāṇḍaṃ ca // 106.05 //
indradhvajanīrājanakhañjanakotpātavarhicitraṃ ca /
puṣyābhiṣekapaṭṭapramāṇam asilakṣaṇaṃ vāstu // 106.06 //
udakārgalam ārāmikam amarālayalakṣaṇaṃ kuliśalepaḥ /
pratimā vanapraveśaḥ surabhavanānāṃ pratiṣṭhā ca // 106.07 //
cihnaṃ gavām atha śunām kukkuṭakūrmājapuruṣacihnaṃ ca /
pañcamanuṣyavibhāgaḥ strīcihnaṃ vastravicchedaḥ // 106.08 //
cāmaradaṇḍaparīkṣā strīstotraṃ cāpi subhagakaraṇaṃ ca /
kāndarpikānulepanapuṃstrikādhyāyaśayanavidhiḥ // 106.09 //
vajraparīkṣā mauktikalakṣaṇam atha padmarāgamarakatayoḥ /
dīpasya lakṣaṇaṃ dantadhāvanaṃ śākunaṃ miśram // 106.10 //
antaracakraṃ virutaṃ śvaceṣṭitaṃ virutam atha śivāyāś ca // 106.11 //
caritaṃ mṛgāśvakariṇāṃ vāyasavidyottaraṃ ca tataḥ // 106.11 //
pāko nakṣatraguṇās tithikaraṇaguṇāḥ sadhiṣṇyajanmaguṇāḥ /
gocaram atha grahāṇāṃ kathito nakṣatrapuruṣaś ca // 106.12 //
śatam idam adhyāyānām anuparipāṭikramād anukrāntam /
atra ślokasahasrāṇy ābaddhāny ūnacatvāri // 106.13 //
atraivāntarbhūtaṃ pariśeṣaṃ nigaditaṃ ca yātrāyām /
bahvāścaryaṃ jātakam uktaṃ karaṇaṃ ca bahucodyam // 106.14 //
